Comment: tremontathletic said "Healthy French Toast?
OH YEAH  We didn't even skimp on the syrup!  You'll need:
2 cups almond milk
1 tsp sea salt
1 tsp nutmeg
2 tsp cinnamon
2 tsp vanilla extract
2 cups kefir
4 sprouted whole-grain English muffins, halved
2 bananas, sliced
4 Tbsp shredded coconut
8 tsp maple syrup  1. Preheat oven to 350F. In a bowl, whisk together almond milk, sea salt, nutmeg, cinnamon, vanilla extract, and kefir. 2. Soak English muffin halves in the mixture for 1 to 2 minutes. 3. Place muffins on a baking pan lightly coated in cooking spray, then layer banana slices on top. Bake 30 to 35 minutes. 4. Remove toasts from dish, top with shredded coconut, and se4. Remove toasts from dish, top with shredded coconut, and serve with maple syrup.  Who's ready for brunching?  Grocery courtesy: Blue Sky Green Fields @blueskygreenfields || Recipe courtesy: Women's Health Magazine"

Comment: jonjarc said "Day 39 - sun! What a difference a day makes. What a difference the sun makes. 30 degrees feels like a heat wave! A little melting snow goes a long way to improving your mood. So does nature's anti-depressant, the handstand or headstand. Seriously. There are all sorts of things written about the power of inversions in yoga. Today, we took advantage of both. My good friend and I were feeling a little lost this morning, then decided, when we saw the sun streaming through the skylights, and felt its warmth, we needed to break the pity party and flip it up. Our students all thought we were nuts, which we are, but it definitely changed the dynamic of the day. Made for some fun afternoon classes! Seriously, if you are feeling down, find a buddy, and go hang upside down for a few minutes...you will feel remarkably better. Use a wall, a spotter, whatever it takes...it's worth it for a quick mood booster. Spring is almost here! #getitdone #yogaeverydamnday #365daysofhandstands #turnupwithme #magis #teamwellness #youcandoit #yoga #handstand @christina_stires"
